# big-code-strata-feat-001: Implement CDS Tranche Product in OpenGamma Strata

## Task

Implement a new `CdsTranche` product type for pricing synthetic CDO (Collateralized Debt Obligation) tranches in OpenGamma Strata. A CDS tranche represents a slice of credit risk from a CDS index portfolio, defined by attachment and detachment points that determine the subordination level.

Strata already has CDS (`Cds`, `CdsTrade`, `ResolvedCds`) and CDS Index (`CdsIndex`, `CdsIndexTrade`, `ResolvedCdsIndex`) product types in `modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/`. The tranche product extends this by adding loss absorption boundaries.

The implementation must follow Strata's Joda-Beans pattern and span across the product, pricer, and measure modules:

1. **Product module** (`modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/`):
   - Create `CdsTranche.java` — Joda-Bean with fields: `underlyingIndex` (CdsIndex reference), `attachmentPoint` (double 0.0-1.0), `detachmentPoint` (double 0.0-1.0), `protectionStart`, `buySell`, `currency`, `notional`, `fixedRate`, `paymentSchedule`
   - Create `CdsTrancheTrade.java` — Trade wrapper following `CdsIndexTrade` pattern
   - Create `ResolvedCdsTranche.java` — Resolved form with expanded payment periods

2. **Pricer module** (`modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/`):
   - Create `IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java` — Pricer following `IsdaCdsProductPricer` pattern, computing present value with tranche-specific loss allocation (expected loss between attachment/detachment points)

3. **Measure module** (`modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/`):
   - Create `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java` — Calculation function wiring the tranche into Strata's calc engine, following `CdsTradeCalculationFunction` pattern

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/Strata--66225ca9 (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/Strata--66225ca9 (mirror of OpenGamma/Strata) (Java, ~500K LOC)
- **Category**: Feature Implementation
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: modules/product/credit, modules/pricer/credit, modules/measure/credit

## Requirements

1. Identify all files that need modification to implement this feature
2. Follow existing patterns and conventions in the codebase (Joda-Beans `@BeanDefinition`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`)
3. Implement the feature with actual code changes
4. Ensure the implementation compiles and doesn't break existing functionality

   if (!cds.getProtectionEndDate().isAfter(ratesProvider.getValuationDate())) { //short cut already expired CDSs\n      return 0d;\n    }\n    LocalDate stepinDate = reduceDiscountFactors(cds, ratesProvider);\n\n    PointSensitivityBuilder protectionLegSensi =\n        protectionLegSensitivity(cds, rates.getFirst(), rates.getSecond(), referenceDate, effectiveStartDate, recoveryRate);\n    PointSensitivityBuilder riskyAnnuitySensi =\n        riskyAnnuitySensitivity(cds, rates.getFirst(), rates.getSecond(), referenceDate, stepinDate, effectiveStartDate)\n            .multipliedBy(-cds.getFixedRate());\n\n    return protectionLegSensi.combinedWith(riskyAnnuitySensi);\n  }\n\n com.opengamma.strata.pricer.common.PriceType;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTranche;\n\n/**\n * Pricer for CDS tranche products based on ISDA standard model.\n * <p>\n * A CDS tranche is a slice of a CDS index portfolio, with protection only on losses\n * between the attachment and detachment points.\n * <p>\n * The pricer uses the homogeneous pool assumption on the public Set<Measure> supportedMeasures() {\n    return MEASURES;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Optional<String> identifier(CdsTrancheTrade target) {\n    return target.getInfo().getId().map(id -> CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    // extract data from product\n    CdsTranche tranche = trade.getProduct();\n    CdsIndex index = scenarios for one measure\n    Map<Measure, Result<?>> results = new HashMap<>();\n    for (Measure measure : measures) {\n      results.put(measure, calculate(measure, resolved, marketData, (calculation == null) {\n      return Result.failure(\n          null,\n          null,\n          \"CDS Tranche calculation not supported for measure: \" + measure);\n    }\n\n    try {\n      return calculation.calculate(resolved, marketData, refData);\n    } catch (Exception ex) {\n      return Result.failure(null, ex);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Interface for functions that calculate a single measure.\n   */\n  @FunctionalInterface\n  interface SingleMeasureCalculation {\n\n    /**\n     * Calculates a single measure for a resolved trade.\n     *\n     * @param resolved  the resolved /**
 * Pricer for CDS tranche products based on ISDA standard model.
 * <p>
 * A CDS tranche is a slice of a CDS index portfolio, with protection only on losses
 * between the attachment and detachment points.
 * <p>
 * The pricer uses the homogeneous pool assumption on the underlying index,
 * pricing the tranche as a synthetic instrument with tranche-specific loss allocation.
 */
public class IsdaCdsTranchePricer {

  /**
   * Default implementation.
   */
  public static final IsdaCdsTranchePricer DEFAULT =
      new IsdaCdsTranchePricer(AccrualOnDefaultFormula.ORIGINAL_ISDA);

  /**
   * The pricer for the underlying CDS index.
   */
  private final IsdaHomogenousCdsIndexProductPricer underlyingPricer;

  /**
   * Constructor specifying the formula to use for the accrued on default calculation.
   *
   * @param formula  the formula
   */
  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(AccrualOnDefaultFormula formula) {
    this.underlyingPricer = new IsdaHomogenousCdsIndexProductPricer(formula);
  }

  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------
  /**
   * Gets the accrual-on-default formula used in this pricer.
   *
   * @return the formula
   */
  pu
